 ham bahut khush hai
 I've lived with depression on and off since i was about 13 years old
 This is not a revelation or a confession
 Those who know me know this about me
 It's not something i take any pains to hide, I'm not ashamed of it or particularly troubled by it
 It's just a part of who i am
 i have days where i feel good and then i have days where i don't
 One minute everything's fine and the next it's like someone turned the light off inside my head
 i go quiet and it's difficult to get out of bed
 Like it always does the world around me loses focus and i struggle to make sense of it
 Sometimes these bouts last an hour - sometimes they last days
 Today, I'm on day 4
 i say i live with depression rather than i struggle with it because for me (and i speak only for myself here) i don't see why it has to be a struggle
 i once read an idea by an American essayist called Richard Mitchell which stayed with me; it's now become how i try to approach the dips in my week or month
 The idea is this: To be sick, or to suffer, is inevitable
 But to become bitter and vindictive in sickness and suffering and to surrender to irrationality, supposing yourself the innocent and virtuous victim of the evils intentions of the world, is not inevitable
 The appropriate answer to the question - Why me? is the other question - Why not me? *** Why am i writing about this? Well, i spend a fair amount of time on social media during the course of my day and today i found myself looking for something to post because it's been a few days since I've posted anything
 i couldn't find anything so i figured I'd just talk about this - how I'm doing, instead of what I'm doing
 It's as simple as that, and we could all stand to do a little more of it

 S

 ye us kahani jaisi lagati he jisamen saat andhon ne ek hathi kii alag-alag vyakhya kii thi
 But still it has some subtle elements
 lekin wo sookshm tatv sirf mukherjee ke bhaashan main nahin hai
 He is also in the speech of the Sangh chief and by looking at the two together some concrete things can come out
 dhur hinduvadi log isi se prasann hue ki unhone dow headgavar ko desh kaa mahaan sapoot bataaya or pracheen bharat kii kai vyavasthaaon kii tarif kii to duusari taraf congressi or kuch vampanthi (saare nahin) isliye khush hai ki unhone nehru kaa zikr kiya, samvidhan kii baat kii vagairah-vagairah
 Indeed, these interpretations are one-sided and conveniently selected
 bahultawad, vividhta aadi kii baat to sangh pramukh ne bhi kii or pranab mukherjee ne bhi, lekin ye khabar sangh pramukh ke sandarbh main zyada mahatvapurn he ki unhone vividhta kii baat kii
 However Hinduism or the old Sanatan system did not consider any one system at the level of thought or practice and it was very recently with the rise of the Sangh that an attempt was made to propagate an organization, a unit and a language
 aisa kai baar anya dharmon kaa sa abhas detaa tha jisaki nakal sangh karnaa chahta tha
 In such a situation, talking about diversity or plurality at least repeatedly from such a large and publicized platform of the Sangh chief was an important news of Pranab Babu's visit to Nagpur
 pranab mukherjee ke bhaashan kaa ek pramukh hissaa hindu dharm kii chaashni main duba hua tha
 This was partly according to its direct audience and often factual
 ve hindu dharm ke vishay main kuch-kuch gandhi yaa vivekanand kii baton ko bol rahe the

 The thing to remember is that the political background of Pranab Mukherjee from Bengal is a period of left-supremacy which is also called by many as 'left-terror'
 jaahir he, hindu dharm yaa rashtrawaad kii unase gaiyr-vampanthi vyakhya hi apekshit thi
 In a half-hour speech, Mukherjee could not even say all the things, many things are said in gestures on such forums
 pranab babu ne spasht rup se sweekaar kiya ki 12veen sadi main gori kaa akraman ek muslim aakrantha kaa akraman tha or lagbhag phir 600 saal bharat par musalamaanon kaa raaj rahaa (us aam prachaar ke ulat ki bharat main hajaar saal tak musalamaanon kaa raaj tha!)unhone hindu itihaas par zyada samay kharch kiya jabaki haal kii ghatana hone or spasht tathy uplabdh hone ke baad bhi muslim shashan ke itihaas ko ekaadh pakti main samet diya
 These things must have been liked by the people of the Sangh, but the other side of it is that the period of Muslim rule in the written and written history of almost 5000 years of India is just 600 years and mostly of North India
 to kya unhen apane bhaashan main kam se kam 5-10 fisadi samay us itihaas ko nahin dena chahie tha? haalanki isaki bharpai unhone aadhunik bharat ke samvidhan, gandhi-nehru kaa drushtikon, rabindranath tagore ke uddhran or samasik samskruti kii visheshta ko batalaakar jarur kii, jiske liye ve badhai ke paatr hai
 But, where the Sangh chief and Mukherjee appeared unanimous was the unity in diversity and its power to 'integrate' diverse cultures into Indian culture
 sangh pramukh ne sookshm tareeke se ‚Äòsaajhe purvaj, saajhe lekin sthaneey mahapurush or sabake bharat-putr‚Äô hone kii baat duhara di jisamen ‚Äòbahari purvaj, bahari mahapurush or gaiyr-bharat putr‚Äô ke liye kya sthaan he yah spasht nahin he

 pranab mukherjee ne lakh bahultawad or nehru-gandhi kaa zikr kiya ho, lekin unhone sangh pramukh kii lagbhag unheen baton ko duhara diya or ye anayas nahin he ki unhone madraland yaa aakhir main vandemaataram shabd bhi bolaa

 yah vaktavy darasal vahi vaktavy he jise sangh pramukh sanathan mat kaa pravaah kehete hai or jise secular-libral samooh islam ke aagaman ke pashchaat ganga-jamuni samskruti kaa naam dekar us ‚Äòanwarat pravaah‚Äô ko maanane se inkaar karata he

 bharatiyon kii yah ahmanyata puraani he

 is soch kaa kya khamiyaja desh ko bhugatna padaa, vah vishleshan is lekh kaa makasad nahin he

 kai patrakaron ne likhaa ki pranab ke jane se sangh ko bahut media kawarej mil gaya jo anyathaa nahin miltaa

 aisa pehali baar nahin hua he ki sangh ke manch se kisi gaiyr-sanghee yaa congressi ne jaakar bhaashan diya ho yaa usamen hissaa liya ho

 lekin congress ne apni jis kamajori ko ujagar kar diya wo ye ki abhivyakti kii swatantraaa kii baat karanevaali party ne desh ke ek purv raashtrapati ko samvaad karne se rokane kii harsambhav koshish kii

 pherbadal main kuch party mahasachivon or sachivon ko hataa diya gaya he
